I have been here for decades and when storage solutions took over several years ago they were many updated changes. They painted the whole storage area, added many security cameras and added new bright storage numbers, maps and signage.  The restrooms are always stocked and clean.  The concrete floors are not only sweep on a regular basis, but the concrete is mopped on occasion.  My favorite is the key code gate which allows for longer hours (7AM-7PM) and access during holidays.

The employees here are extremely helpful and very friendly.  They seem to really enjoy working there and always greet me with a smile.

I highly recommend using Storage Solutions for all your storage needs!</text>

<name>Chris Johnson</name>< Review>
The worst. Having been here since 2012, I'll be going elsewhere. The manager fined me $25. for using bad language. I told her I wouldn't pay it...she refused my rent payment. Claimed she couldn't take a partial payment. So I printed the invoice I was sent for the rent and submitted it with a money order. The fine was paid first and then the rent. After I made it clear I would not pay a "swear fine". Especially after I heard her cursing a customer herself. After I made it clear I was only paying the invoice. Now I have a late fee and a lien against my property!!!

Fortunately, I am a U.S. Navy veteran and one of our benefits is pro bono legal advice. I intend to small claim both Storage Solutions and her personally.

I can give you other reasons You don't want to rent here...
It's illegal to store flammable liquids in a unit, probably a fire hazard. Manager allows a landscaper to store his gas-powered tools in the facility. With gas tanks. Talk about not caring about all of the other customers at risk.
Manager tells potential customers insurance is mandated by the state. Oops, no it isn't.Storage Solutions requires it because they get a kickback from the insurance company.
They raise the rent every year by the maximum allowed by law...although I have heard some tenants complain it was more than once a year. In my case, they raised it one month before the anniversary date. When brought to Managers attention, she stuttered for an answer. Told me she would get back to me. She didn't.
You might think twice about renting here. There are lower priced, more convenient storage rentals.< /Review>

<username>Trista Owens<//username><Time>1513712380356</Time>< rate>

<review>Dr. Cooper and the staff at Banderas Pet Hospital were absolutely wonderful! This was our first visit to the hospital and it was a visit I was terribly nervous about. A couple years ago, our family lost our 11-yr old furry family member after a long, difficult fight with cancer. While our veterinarian at the time went above and beyond what we could have expected to help our mutt, we felt that perhaps the treatments/surgeries recommended to us toward the end may have been too extreme (that they may have been in over their heads so-to-speak).

As such, after recently finding a mass on our 5-yr old hound, you can imagine how upset and worried we were. I looked at the reviews for many vets around South Orange County, including any references to people dealing with something similar to what we went through with our last dog, and Banderas Pet Hospital seemed like a good option.

The moment we walked in the front door, we felt right at home. The front office staff was extremely friendly to me and kind/loving to our hound. The waiting room was very clean with treats and water for pets and coffee, water and candy for pet-parents. We were taken into the room quickly, the technician was great with our dog (offering treats and loving on and complimenting our boy:)), and we didn't wait long for the doctor. When Dr. Cooper came into the room, she offered our boy a different kind of treat (he didn't like the first one the tech offered him) and proceeded to love on him and listen to my concerns at length. Due to my previous experience with masses/cancer, I was somewhat emotional and worried, but Dr. Cooper was patient and listened to all I had to say. She thoroughly examined our boy and said the mass didn't feel like it would be cancerous but she would take a quick needle sample and review it right then and there. They took a sample and reviewed it in a matter of minutes and Dr. Cooper told us it looked to be a fatty tumor (according to the sample under the microscope, there were no abnormal cells) and told us to keep an eye on it and let her know if the mass grew at a quick pace or if we noticed anything else out of the ordinary. She did not try to up-sell us on anything (i.e. tell us we should send it to the lab just to be safe, we should run more tests, etc.) Basically, if the mass grew at a worrisome pace or changed composition (i.e. changed shape, became more solid, etc.) to bring him back and they'd run more tests at that time.

Basically, Dr. Cooper seemed to understand that, with all we had gone through with our last dog, we weren't eager to put our current dog through a mess of testing/surgeries/etc. Also, it is important to mention that cost was not a primary concern for us (we have pet insurance for things like this), but it was nice not to be pushed to buy unnecessary services. As we were leaving, the tech and receptionist continued to compliment and love our boy up and checked us out in a timely fashion. I couldn't be happier with their service.< /review>< pictures>
None< /pictures>

< Review>
This is the best Mexican food in Granada Hills, Northridge, Reseda, Tarzana, basically within 50 miles.  The food is freshly cooked and always amazing.  The salsa is the real goldmine here, it is spicy, hot (but low impact tongue burn for the thick red sauce, which is the BEST) but probably the best tasting and most satisfying salsa I have had!!!   Beef crispy tacos and steak quesadillas are great but our all time favorite is the chicken/rice/cheese (only) burrito. It is a monster and oh so yummy.< /Review>

Food is EXCELLENT.

The owner (an Asian lady) is wonderful...

the other women (a slightly heavy set Latina)

is NOT (the main reason why deducted 1-star from this review.)

The hard shell chicken tacos are BOMB! They taste homemade...

...the menudo, better than the Juanita's can bought at Von's or Ralph's or any other local Mexican restaurant.

...the carne asada TASTE like carne asada, not some beef flank.

...and the torta, WOW. Talk about HUGE. Well worth the price.

If you're hungry for AUTHENTIC Mexican food at a fairly decent price (the food can be a bit pricey from time to time depending on what you order)

give this place a chance.  You'll be pleasantly surprised. üòÅ</review>

< Review>
This is the best place to get Mexican food in the valley.   We have been going there since they opened.  All of the staff are always friendly,  and willing to customize my food to fit my dietary needs.  The food is authentic and not super salty.  Their green tomatillo salsa is AMAZING.   The portions are generous,  cooked to perfection, and their prices are way reasonable.   The place is a little hole in the wall,  that does have a walk up ordering counter and several tables to dine in. This restaurant is definitely worth driving all the way across the valley when we have a craving for mexican food.  Be ready to wait a few minutes, if they are busy.  They have a small staff, and cook all of the food to order.< /Review>

I went to Old Navy today to return an item and I saw jeans for $10!! I didn't walk around because they were right by the line ... I thought yaaay, score!!!!
While in line in front of me a young lady was telling Michael "manager" that the price was incorrect. So he goes and checks it out and honors the price... Great!
My turn... Both the pants I picked (off the $10 rack) were not $10. Mind you, there was more than one of the same kind I picked on the rack, but different sizes!!
I proceed to tell Kathryn, the young lady helping me that they should honor the price because they were on the $10 rack!
Well, Michael "manager" said no. It really bummed me out! Why did he honor the young ladies items but not mine!?
I feel that was very unfair and I will be contacting corporate. I run a store, and I would rather honor a $5 price difference than loss $10 and a customer.
Michael is not a very good manager.<//review>

<Gmap_id>0x80dd4ac185590e89:0xb0bc1df5728aafcb</Gmap_id><Date>1526952092733</Date><name>Kevin Hinton</name><UserId.>106975532374096173834<//UserId.></record>

< Name>
Grace Loundou<//Name>
<Time>1565881301052< /Time><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
LOVE this place, I first visited quite a few years ago and haven't been back up until about a month ago when I was craving an Acai bowl. This is the closest and most convenient location near home. Parking lot is small and may be packed during peak times since it's shared with several other dining businesses.

I love to order the guarana bowl in the small size (24oz) or the large size (32oz) if I'm particularly hungry. Small bowl some with one topping of choice, bananas, granola, honey. Large size comes with two toppings of choice and every else that's standard with small size. I like how everything pairs well together and are all the right proportions. The Blends are fruity and not icy as all as they don't dilute it with ice.

Prices are fair for what you get, just be aware that Acai bowls run on the pricey side in general - a little under or over $10 depending on what you get and what size.

Wait time for bowl to be ready sometimes takes awhile, so be prepared to wait if it's particularly busy.<//Review>

< Text>
Whenever I go to an acai bowl place, it's a hit or miss. Mostly because the bowls are too big for me to finish or that it's too sweet. But when I walked into Beach Bowls, I was happy to see a large menu with a mini bowl option.
So I went with a mini bowl which has a base of acai, banana, honey and granola but I added vanilla power ( has 18g protein) and mangos.
Upon receiving the bowl, I devoured it and it was delicious. It was fruity and fresh. I wish they had coconut shavings but that's about it. I don't have
a photo mainly because I was hungry and it was hot and I really wanted to eat the thing.
So if you want an acai bowl, go here.< /Text>
